msg:Advantages: The location is very good. Downstairs is Beiguo Mall and Letai Center. There is a subway entrance and Chang'an Park nearby. It is very convenient for eating and shopping. There is free underground parking. Hotel guests can use the swimming pool for free. The swimming pool is also good, with standard swimming lanes and quite spacious. The executive suite we stayed in was very large and had newer facilities. There were two toilets, a spacious bathroom, and a floor-to-ceiling window in the living room. You can sit in front of the window and watch the night view of the street, which is also good. The bath water is good. It is quite comfortable to stay.
I hope it can be better: 1. I originally booked a suite to add a bed for the child to sleep. It doesn't matter if it is charged. It is OK according to the hotel introduction when booking. However, after checking in, I was told that no extra bed could be added. I don't know if it is because of the shortage of staff during holidays. However, the housekeeper gave us a set of bedding. We put the sofas in the living room together and we could sleep. It still helped solve the problem. 2. The management brother in the swimming pool was a bit rough. My husband went to swim at the beginning, and I took the children in afterwards. I didn't want to swim that day, and the children were also hesitant, so I wanted to sit on the bench for a while, and then go down to change clothes when I wanted to swim. At that time, there was another family sitting by the swimming pool in casual clothes. My child and I were about to walk in from the entrance, and then we were yelled at by the swimming pool manager. Yes, yelled, asking us what we were doing. I was holding the key and towel I got at the front desk at the time. I said we wanted to swim, but the children were hesitant, so we went in and sat for a while. The big brother said that we were not allowed to sit in if we didn't swim, and then saw me looking at another person sitting in casual clothes, and immediately changed his words and said that only hotel guests could go in and sit in casual clothes. I said I was a hotel guest, and the big brother said that you can go in. In fact, I think that we understand the management rules of the hotel, but we don't know. You can come over and ask where we are from first, and then tell us the rules. There is no need to yell directly. There were no more than 10 guests in the swimming pool at that time, and you were not busy. You will always talk nicely. 3. We checked out on the morning of the day we left the hotel, and paid for breakfast at the front desk. As a result, the hotel called again at around 4 pm to ask if we wanted to extend our stay. I said I had already checked out. The other party was very surprised and asked me where I put the room card. I said I gave it to the front desk. Then the other party didn't explain anything and hung up the phone directly. At that time, the hotel housekeeper was still urging me to give a five-star rating, and I had to remember to send her a screenshot after the rating. I was instantly in a bad mood. To be honest, I am not a serious person. The hotel facilities are really good, and I know that the staff's work is not easy, but to be honest, the overall service experience of staying in the hotel is not very good, and I always feel controlled by the staff. It can be regarded as a flaw in staying in the hotel.
In summary, the hotel's supporting facilities are very good and cost-effective, but I hope that the service details can be done better. The service of a good hotel should be very comfortable and considerate, rather than sending fruit snacks and asking for a five-star rating directly. It is interacting with guests attentively, rather than relying on some marketing methods to force it out. I hope Ximei will get better and better.
